		name_list_anglo_norse = cn_britain_danish # Bretland		

	}
	
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_west_germanic
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_goidelic
					has_cultural_pillar = heritage_brythonic
				}
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}

		can_create = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					is_ai = yes
				}
				culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_brythonic }
			}
		}
		
		ai_primary_priority = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = culture:welsh
				}
				add = @correct_culture_primary_score
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						culture = culture:cumbrian
						culture = culture:cornish
						culture = culture:breton
					}
				}
				add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
			}
		}

			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = culture:cornish

			}

				limit = {
					OR = {
						culture = culture:welsh
						culture = culture:cumbrian
						culture = culture:breton
					}
				}
				add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
			}
		}

e_france = {
	color = { 11 22 170 }

	capital = c_ile_de_france

	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = culture:french
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					culture = culture:norman
					culture = culture:occitan
				}
			}
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}

			limit = {

			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
			add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
		}
	}
